   guṇībhūtavyaṅgyākhyākāvyabhedāntaḥ pāto 'nāsvādyatvāt vyaṅgyasya, siṃ	guNIBUta-vyaFgI-A-AKyA-kAvyaBeda-antar pAtaH anAsvAdya-tvAt vyaFgyasya, siM
   tvavarjanīyasannidhitvamātreṇāvasthiteḥ /	tu-avarjanIya-sanniDi-tva-mAtreNa-avasTiteH /
        ata eva kavipratibhāsaṃrambhagocaratvaṃ teṣu nāstīti vācyam /	atas eva kavi-pratiBA-saMramBa-gocara-tvam tezu na-asti-iti vAcyam /
        vānīrakuñje ityādau vyaṅgyasya nānāsvādyatvam, kintu vācyāpekṣayā	vAnIra-kuQje iti-AdO vyaFgyasya nAnA-svAdya-tvam, kintu vAcya-apekzayA
   āsvādapakarṣa iti teṣu ucito guṇībhūtavyaṅgyākhyakāvyavyavahāraḥ /	AsvAdapakarzaH iti tezu ucitaH guNIBUta-vyaFgyA-AKya-kAvya-vyavahAraH /
        kathaṃ ca dhvaniguṇībhūtavyaṅgyayoralaṅkāreṣvantarbhāvaḥ,	kaTam ca Dvani-guNIBUta-vyaFgyayoH-alaFkArezu-antarBAvaH,
   tayoraṅgitvāt /	tayoH-aFgi-tvAt /
        alaṅkāraṇāṃ ca tadaṅgabhūtaśabdārthāśritatvāt /	alaFkAraNAm ca tad-aFga-BUta-Sabda-arTa-ASrita-tvAt /
        taduktaṃ dhvanikṛtā eva---	tat-uktam Dvani-kRtAH eva---
        "aṅgāśritāstvalaṅkārāḥ mantavyāḥ kaṭakādivat" //	"aFga-ASritAH-tu-alaFkArAH mantavyAH kawaka-Adi-vat" //
        ityalaṃ bahunā /	iti-alam bahunA /
        iti śrīsāhityadarpaṇalocane caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ /	iti SrI-sAhitya-darpaNa-locane caturTaH paricCedaH /

   iti sāhityadarpaṇe dhvaniguṇībhūtavyaṅgyākhyakāvyabhedanirūpaṇo nāma	iti sAhitya-darpaNe DvaniguNIBUtavyaFgyAKyakAvyaBedanirUpaNaH nAma
